</a> <br/>Lana McDaniel<a href='http://s1293.beta.photobucket.com/user/booksandpoems/media/Lana2_zps97c23188.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410315i/804396._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo Lana2_zps97c23188.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><u>
  <i>Synopsis:</i>
</u>Sawyer Vincent is still heartbroken over his breakup with Ashton Grey. Things are made even worse by the fact that he lost his girl to his brother, and now the pair are ridiculously happy while he's all alone. But Lana McDaniel thinks she might just have a cure. Lana's lived in her cousin Ashton's shadow all her life, but now she's taking the lead and is determined to make Sawyer her man. But can she be sure that Sawyer's not just using her to ge</span>
  <span id="freeText11778183994570778761" style="display:none">Sawyer Vincent <a href="http://s1293.beta.photobucket.com/user/booksandpoems/media/Sawyer_zps315ad495.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410315i/804395._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo Sawyer_zps315ad495.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <br>Lana McDaniel<a href="http://s1293.beta.photobucket.com/user/booksandpoems/media/Lana2_zps97c23188.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410315i/804396._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo Lana2_zps97c23188.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><u>
  <i>Synopsis:</i>
</u>Sawyer Vincent is still heartbroken over his breakup with Ashton Grey. Things are made even worse by the fact that he lost his girl to his brother, and now the pair are ridiculously happy while he's all alone. But Lana McDaniel thinks she might just have a cure. Lana's lived in her cousin Ashton's shadow all her life, but now she's taking the lead and is determined to make Sawyer her man. But can she be sure that Sawyer's not just using her to get back at Ashton?<br> <br>The Vincent Brothers is the second book in the Vincent Boys series ( i believe there aren't going to be anymore books). It starts 6 months later from where we left of in The Vincent Boys, and it has both Sawyer's and Lana's POV. <br><br>I'll be honest, i was not overexcited about reading The Vincent Brothers after finding out it focuses entirely on Sawyer and his story. I mean, we <u>do</u> still see a bit of Beau and Ashton too, but not as much as i would have liked. And the main reason why i wasn't very excited, might be because i do not like Sawyer, neither do i really like Lana. Yep, that is a big problem.<br><br><b><blockquote>"You touch a place inside of me that Ashton never did. I feel things with you, i never felt for her..."</blockquote> </b><br><br>I found Sawyer to be a massive jerk, at the end of book 1, and in this one as well. He was using Lana to forget about Ashton, and that was nerve racking for me. Plus he was <i>blaming</i> Beau, for stealing his perfect life, and for getting everything he had always wanted. I seriously wanted to punch him in the freaking face. I mean, Beau <i>FOUGHT</i> for every little thing he got. Sawyer just had it on his plate! He had great, rich parents, who loved him ,while Beau was living in a shit hole with <i> white trash parents.</i> That stupid boy, Sawyer, had the<i>nerve</i> to say Beau stole his life. Ahh!<br><a href="http://www.sherv.net/3d.mad-emoticon-249.html" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img alt="3D smiley full of anger" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/198335.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <blockquote> "Mine," Sawyer said in a fierce voice before he grabbed my hips and begun controlling my movements. " You're mine. All mine. You're so wet." <blockquote></blockquote>
</blockquote>
</b><br><br>Lana was just too desperate to get Sawyer. I don't like girls like her. And i hate it that she changed her appearance, and her fashion mainly because if him. He should have loved her because of who she is, not because of the way she looks. But i think he actually managed to do the former at the end.<br><br>Sawyer's and Lana's relationship was progressing a little bit too fast. Mrs Glines should take her time with her books, maybe that way she will improve them in the process too.<br><br>The sex scenes where not as good as in the previous book. I'm not even sure if Lana lost her virginity yet! Thought they did do some pretty hot stuff.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>"... When you fall for the one that owns you, she will be the only one who has power to make you cry."</blockquote>
</b> <br><br>I seem to only talk about the bad things, lol. Don't get me wrong, i really enjoyed this book. It was great. There were many romantic, fun, and passionate scenes that i just adored. I absolutely loved the friendships, and the family problems the characetrs were facing. I think what i most enjoyed was the way Abbi Glines writes her leading men, and the way she nailed the Southern temperament. She is <i> fantastic</i> at those two things.<br><br>Now comes the best part - The ending! I don't think i have ever read an ending as great as in The Vincent Brothers. I did not even expect it to be good, but it was so much more than that! It was marvelous, and it had me squealing till the very last page! Loved it!<br><br>And they all lived happily ever after - awww<br><a href="http://myniceprofile.com/movies-147894.html" title="Movies Comments Pictures" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380410315ra/804397.gif" alt="Movies Comments Pictures" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="http://myniceprofile.com/" title="Movies Comments Pictures" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><b> <blockquote>"Lana. I think about you every minute of every day. When i'm with you my world is complete. When i lost you, i completely shattered. You. Own. Me." </blockquote></b> <br><br>Overall, The Vincent Brothers was a very enjoyable read. Even though i did not like Sawyer, i think he is alright now, same goes for Lana. What can i say? Sawyer definitely <i> <u>CAN NOT </u> </i> compete with Beau. This book pulled my heart in all the right places. I recommend this to Abbi Glines fans, readers who love romance with drama, and mature readers. </span>
  <a data-text-id="11778183994570778761" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1966947233" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1966947233" />
    <a title="Talía" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16352870-tal-a"><img alt="Talía" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1539391978p2/16352870.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1966947233?book_show_action=true">Apr 09, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Talía" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Talía" href="/user/show/16352870-tal-a">Talía</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16352870-tal-a?shelf=read-2017">read-2017</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1966947233" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3653962898316579103"><b>2.9 - 3 Moving On STARS</b><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I know this because I understand now what love really feels like. The kind that consumes you. Love holds the power to break you. It holds the power to complete you.” </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/>For some reason this year I`ve been reading a lot of this teen angst trash books (trash in the sense that they`re addictive but not really well developed), maybe is because I need something light to read with all the stress recently from college. Anyways, I needed something and I stumble upon this</span>
  <span id="freeText3653962898316579103" style="display:none"><b>2.9 - 3 Moving On STARS</b><br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I know this because I understand now what love really feels like. The kind that consumes you. Love holds the power to break you. It holds the power to complete you.” </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br />For some reason this year I`ve been reading a lot of this teen angst trash books (trash in the sense that they`re addictive but not really well developed), maybe is because I need something light to read with all the stress recently from college. Anyways, I needed something and I stumble upon this one and I just gave it a go. I actually read the first book years ago and I didn’t reread it this time around, but I didn’t struggle as much as I expected.<br /><br /><b>Sawyer Vincent</b> is the golden boy. The one who’s smart and has a bright future all planned out. But after losing his girlfriend and childhood best friend Ashton to his cousin Beau, he feels crushed. He loves them both, but six months is still no time enough to move on from the girl you thought the one. <br /><b>Lana McDaniel</b> has always known that Sawyer was the one for her. For years she has lived under the perfect shadow of her cousin Ashton, and even facing the fact Ash got the guy she fell for. But now that not only Sawyer is single but her body has caught up to a more womanly version, Lana will find that maybe her time has come to act on those feelings. <b>
  <u>And this summer will change everything.</u>
</b><br /><blockquote>
  <i>“Ashton grinne and raised her eyebrows. "I can't believe you're telling me a Vincent boy brought you to Grove, Alabama and not me."<br />Shrugging, I returned her smile. "They're heard to resist."<br />"Don't I know it.”</i>
</blockquote><br />I’m kinda disappointed. <u>The story felt immature, with some super cheesy lines and the characters didn’t developed that much.</u><br />Sawyer was a jerk through much of the book, he didn’t care much for his friends and I know he was hurting but I just didn’t care much for him. He had a charming side and I did enjoy it when he left that burned side of himself back to focus on Lana.<br />Lana was likeable, but I disliked the fact that she somewhat was relevant now because she was “hot”. It felt like an excuse to backup the reasons why now her and Sawyer could be a thing, more than her having an actual chemistry or building something genuine with him.<br /><blockquote>
  <b>“When you fall for the one that owns you, she’ll be the only one that has the power to make you cry.”</b>
</blockquote><br />Sawyer and Lana’s relationship was rocky, it either was good or bad. I felt that I never got the point where Sawyer started focusing on Lana and moving on from Ashton, and I wished there was an explicit point to it because I wasn’t sure of his actions. Their relationship had some pretty cute moments and I did see they could be good together, but I didn`t totally buy it either.<br /><br />As for secondary characters, Beau was so problematic with his overprotective behavior over Ashton, like he seriously didn’t allow people to look at her bad or even say one thing that wasn’t overly good. He fought for everything and didnt allow Ash to stand up for herself more and freaking trust her to just be with him. But i did notice he was the most loyal person and his relationship with Sawyer was interesting, so at the end I wasn`t as annoyed with him. To be honest, I don’t remember much of Ash in the first book, so idk if she’s acting just the same, but I hoped for her to be more independent of Beau as a person, and that didn’t happen.<br /><blockquote>
  <i>“Sawyer was always the Vincent boy worth fighting for.<br />He's the special one.” </i>
</blockquote><br />I disliked the first 15 chapters, but then the story got better when discovering Lana’s struggles, which added a dimension to her I enjoyed. I felt her struggle to be loved and not being second best, and also seeing how your dreams seem to be falling apart. I liked she realized at some point she didn’t deserve Sawyer to threat her like second option, and even though her actions were a bit childish, I felt she had the more development and that at least gave the story more layers.<br /><br />Overall, I read this so fast because, even though I wasnt that into it, I was enjoying seeing what would happen. <u>I know this is not a masterpiece, but I needed something light, fun and teen angst, and this definitely met the expectations.</u></span>
  <a data-text-id="3653962898316579103" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_297731741" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/297731741" />
    <a title="Gitte TotallyBookedBlog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7379751-gitte-totallybookedblog"><img alt="Gitte TotallyBookedBlog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514886578p2/7379751.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/297731741?book_show_action=true">Mar 20, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Gitte TotallyBookedBlog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Gitte TotallyBookedBlog" href="/user/show/7379751-gitte-totallybookedblog">Gitte TotallyBookedBlog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer297731741" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15740039982710948327">"When you fall for the one who owns you, she'll be the only one that has the power to make you cry" - Beau...*sigh*<br/><br/>WOW...I am in my happy place right now...I LOVE LOVE LOVED <br/>The Vincent Brothers!! This was a PERFECT sequel..and I have to say I read it in one sitting because I cannot get enough of the Vincent Brothers and THAT accent which I hear in my head clear as day and that has a piece of my heart!!<br/><br/><b>Shhh</b> ...whispering...<br/>(I think this one might just be my fave and my ♥ belonged completely to B</span>
  <span id="freeText15740039982710948327" style="display:none">"When you fall for the one who owns you, she'll be the only one that has the power to make you cry" - Beau...*sigh*<br /><br />WOW...I am in my happy place right now...I LOVE LOVE LOVED <br />The Vincent Brothers!! This was a PERFECT sequel..and I have to say I read it in one sitting because I cannot get enough of the Vincent Brothers and THAT accent which I hear in my head clear as day and that has a piece of my heart!!<br /><br /><b>Shhh</b> ...whispering...<br />(I think this one might just be my fave and my ♥ belonged completely to Beau before but now ♥ ♥ Sawyer ♥ ♥ !!)<br /><br />The Vincent Brothers picks up 6 months after the break-up of Sawyer and Ashton. Sawyer is still hurt, heartbroken, and angry trying to come to terms with seeing them together every day and adjusting to the fact that his brother is with the girl he loves.(In the Vincent Boys, Sawyer and Ashton broke up after she fell in love with Beau and him with her.)<br /><br />We didn't really get to know the "real" Sawyer all that well in the first book and I have to admit that because we saw him through Ashton and Beau's eyes I kind of disliked him..alot..(I feel really bad now!!). However, in The Vincent Brothers we get to hear Sawyer's voice and see things from his perspective and get how he felt about what happened with Beau and Ashton. I LOVED that! It made him real and it put his behavior into perspective! I loved getting to know Lana too as in the previous book she was there but didn't really leave much of an impression on me as a side character.<br /><br />So...Sawyer and Lana's journey begins when they "bump" into each other on a night out. Lana, Ashtons cousin, is there for the summer and is staying with Ashton. Lana has changed her appearance over the last six months in order to finally get Sawyer to notice her, as she has long been in love with him - <br /><br />"Sawyer was always the Vincent boy worth fighting for. He's the special one" - Lana<br /><br />Sawyer does indeed notice Lana, but unfortunately he has plans to use her as a way to make Ashton jealous and as a summer distraction for himself. His plan, (which made me pretty mad!!!) doesn't quite go as well as expected though when Lana gets to him in a way that not even Ashton did. I LOVED Lana because despite her sad personal circumstances which should have knocked her down; she stood up for herself, she was feisty, she knew what she was worth and didn't take any nonsense. Just what Sawyer needs!!! And Sawyer *sigh* he really got me mad at times but he totally redeemed himself and this one scene (won't spoil it) had me in tears and I felt all emotional!!! When Sawyer loves...he LOVES!!!<br /><br />I LOVED the epilogue too..I'm a sucker for epilogues and this one - PERFECT!!!!<br /><br />I feel kind of sad now that it's over but happy and satisfied too..(I am hoping that it doesn't end here though ;0). <br /><br />This series is amazing and I can't recommend it and Abbi Glines enough!!!<br /><br /><br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="15740039982710948327" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer1254016771467992958">Uncut & Extended version<br/><br/>This book was about Sawyer and Lana<br/><br/> <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380416449i/822481._SX540_.jpg' width='' height='' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Lana has loved Sawyer since they were kids. <i>"Sawyer was always the Vincent boy worth fight for. He's the special one."</i><br/><br/>This is the conclusion to the Vincent Boy's story. The <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/577227819' rel='nofollow noopener'>first book</a> had more steam than this books. The first book is still my favorite of the two books.<br/><br/><b>SERIES:</b><br/><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16160996.The_Vincent_Boys_Extended_and_Uncut__The_Vincent_Boys___1_' title='The Vincent Boys Extended and Uncut (The Vincent Boys, #1) by Abbi Glines' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1353409910s/16160996.jpg' alt='The Vincent Boys Extended and Uncut (The Vincent Boys, #1) by Abbi Glines' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16172249.The_Vincent_Brothers_Extended_and_Uncut__The_Vincent_Boys___2_' title='The Vincent Brothers Extended and Uncut (The Vincent Boys, #2) by Abbi Glines' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1369466489s/16172249.jpg' alt='The Vincent Brothers Extended and Uncut (The Vincent Boys, #2) by Abbi Glines' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/>No cliffhanger. Spinoff</span>
  <span id="freeText1254016771467992958" style="display:none">Uncut &amp; Extended version<br><br>This book was about Sawyer and Lana<br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380416449i/822481._SX540_.jpg" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Lana has loved Sawyer since they were kids. <i>"Sawyer was always the Vincent boy worth fight for. He's the special one."</i><br><br>This is the conclusion to the Vincent Boy's story. The <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/577227819" rel="nofollow noopener">first book</a> had more steam than this books. The first book is still my favorite of the two books.<br><br><b>SERIES:</b><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16160996.The_Vincent_Boys_Extended_and_Uncut__The_Vincent_Boys___1_" title="The Vincent Boys Extended and Uncut (The Vincent Boys, #1) by Abbi Glines" rel="nofollow noopener">

<span id="freeTextContainer16253121009647995240"><b>*********************3.5/5*********************<br/><br/>I hated this book just like I hated the one that came before it.<br/>And by <i>hated</i>, I mean 50-50 loved and despised the story because again, Abbi Glines wrote a story that seemed wrong at all the right places and made me ache for her heroine this time!!!<br/><br/>She was able to bring about the dark side of the angelic Vincent boy - <i><u>Sawyer Vincent</u></i>.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1464854445i/19283680._SY540_.jpg' width=' ' height=' ' alt='s' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>- and damn was he <i>hot</i> !!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!<br/><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1464854445ra/19283681.gif' width=' ' height=' ' alt='s' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/>- he proved all of us who thinks he's the goody-two-shoes guy among him and Beau </b></span>
  <span id="freeText16253121009647995240" style="display:none"><b>*********************3.5/5*********************<br><br>I hated this book just like I hated the one that came before it.<br>And by <i>hated</i>, I mean 50-50 loved and despised the story because again, Abbi Glines wrote a story that seemed wrong at all the right places and made me ache for her heroine this time!!!<br><br>She was able to bring about the dark side of the angelic Vincent boy - <i><u>Sawyer Vincent</u></i>.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1464854445i/19283680._SY540_.jpg" width=" " height=" " alt="s" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>- and damn was he <i>hot</i> !!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!<br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1464854445ra/19283681.gif" width=" " height=" " alt="s" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>- he proved all of us who thinks he's the goody-two-shoes guy among him and Beau wrong!<br>- he seemed <i><s>dark &amp; (sexy!)</s></i><br><br><s><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[SHIT WHEN DID SAWYER VINCENT TURN INTO A SEX GOD !!?!?!?! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></s><br><br>Anyway, moving on...<br><br>It really bothered me that every time the story's being told in Sawyer's perspective, he never fails to mention <s>Ashton</s>. It annoyed me. I had too much of Ashton and Beau already I'm tired of their dramas. Cut me some slack. What I wanna read now was Lana and Sawyer's story!!!!<br><br>At first Sawyer wanted to get back at Ashton and try to make her jealous by using Lana. <br>Sawyer turns Beau-ish by this time and he gets all dark and sexy as he spends time with Lana.<br><br>Lana knows that what she shares with Sawyer could just be a ploy for Ash to go back to Sawyer's arms. But she shook this thought off every damn time it crosses her mind because she's just head over heels in love with Sawyer (ever since!).<br><br>AND EVERY DAMN TIME I ROOTED FOR LANA TO WAKE UP AND STOP BEING SUCH A MARTYR!<br><br>I FEEL THE PAIN!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1445369634ra/16638890.gif" width=" " height=" " alt="S" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>I hate that girls in books never realize that being martyrs just end up with them being hurt and the guys just get to enjoy hurting them more through this. UGH!<br><br>It just pained me to read that Lana always forgives Sawyer for being stupid and for choosing Ashton over her all the time! <br><br>Lana:<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1464854445ra/19283682.gif" width=" " height=" " alt="s" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>idk but i really enjoyed hating Sawyer all through out hahahahah</b></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

  <span id="freeText12863756352794789510" style="display:none">Quick review:<br /><br /><b>Cover:</b> Eye catching<br /><b> Rating: </b> NC-17<br /><b> Thumbs Up: </b> 4<br /><b>Overall:</b> A good follow up to the first book<br /><b>Characters:</b> Good<br /><b>Plot:</b> A lot of drama, a little heat and ending that left me wanting<br /><b>Page Turner:</b> Yes<br /><b> Series Cont.?</b> If there is more to come<br /><b> Recommend: </b> Yes<br /><b>Book Boyfriend:</b> Beau but I’ll pick Sawyer<br /><br /><b>SUMMARY</b> (50 words or less)<br /><br />I like drama and this book had it in spades. In fact things got a little heated too bad they fizzled out way to soon without much follow through. That really was my only complaint. The story was certainly entertaining. <span id="freeTextContainer5417068007800544018"><b>4½ Stars<br/></b>I <i>strongly</i> disliked the first in the series and I felt maybe I was just too old for the YA drama but I actually <i>really</i> liked this one.   <span id="freeText5417068007800544018" style="display:none"><b>4½ Stars<br /></b>I <i>strongly</i> disliked the first in the series and I felt maybe I was just too old for the YA drama but I actually <i>really</i> liked this one. Such a sweet epilogue and Lana was a sweet little cutie pie. <b> Remember those day of wanting someone but he was mooning over someone else.</b> (ahhh, those days;p) Now, Sawyer had me all over the place. Loved him one moment then despised him for using poor Lana. He was upside down, topsy turvy, then up, then sideways, and I finally loved him. Whew! Abbi Glines has been stepping it up lately! Go girl :) </span>

    <a title="DKristin" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6655835-dkristin"><img alt="DKristin" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1495583446p2/6655835.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/456251767?book_show_action=true">Nov 14, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="DKristin" class="user" itemprop="url" name="DKristin" href="/user/show/6655835-dkristin">DKristin</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6655835-dkristin?shelf=own-a-copy">own-a-copy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer456251767" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12519578024437476934">I give this one 2.75 stars... Let's be honest here. I've said it before and I'll probably say it again: Abbi Glines has reached a height where she could write a book about a crackhead taking a dump in an alley and we would gobble that shit right up!!! *Lovely Visual Right?* It's true though. Abbi Glines books are like mashed potatoes. It's something you know which makes it comforting. It's going to fill you up. You don't have to worry about it upsetting your stomach and it's always tasty. <br/><br/>We alr</span>
  <span id="freeText12519578024437476934" style="display:none">I give this one 2.75 stars... Let's be honest here. I've said it before and I'll probably say it again: Abbi Glines has reached a height where she could write a book about a crackhead taking a dump in an alley and we would gobble that shit right up!!! *Lovely Visual Right?* It's true though. Abbi Glines books are like mashed potatoes. It's something you know which makes it comforting. It's going to fill you up. You don't have to worry about it upsetting your stomach and it's always tasty. <br /><br />We already know that there is going to be a boy and a girl they'll fall madly in love. One or both of them will be jacked up in some way and one or both of them will unintentionally continue to push the other away when they could have been with each other the entire time. They'll work it out, make up, HEA. This book was no different. I bought it because it was finally on sale for 1.99 a price that I thought was reasonable based off of what I read in the first book in the series. Don't get me wrong I liked this. I read it because I knew it would be light and easy to digest. I really liked Lana and a lot of the things that she said about her relationships especially with her parents really hit home. She was definitely dealt a crap hand and it felt good to see her keep pushing forward despite it. I thought it was interesting how moronic Sawyer could be but then at other times give others like his Dad words of wisdom... Go figure. Beau and Ashton were there normal self-absorbed selves nothing new. Definitely had a HEA. So if you're in the mood for risotto or linguine in garlic sauce move along but if you want some good old mashed potatoes this is the book for you! Especially while it is on sale!!! </span>
  <a data-text-id="12519578024437476934" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer15180515444948491473">It’s over, I’m so sad! :( I’m going to miss the amazing Vincent Boys. I wasn’t sure if I would like The Vincent Brothers, since it was Lana and Sawyers story. I loved it! Who knew Sawyer had a little bad boy in him? There were a couple of yummy Sawyer scenes I needed an industrial fan to cool myself off with. :) I always thought Sawyer and Lana would be perfect for each other and they are. I’m REALLY going to miss this series and these characters. Also the epilogue was perfect!</span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer533039094" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1215393635901865815"><b>2 1/2 to 3 stars</b><br/><br/>Nothing particularly wrong with this book other than it's too Young Adult and cliched for me. If you like the Young Adult genre you'll probably enjoy this story.<br/></span>

          </span>
        </div>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_430772977" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/430772977" />
    <a title="Alexa" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1894085-alexa"><img alt="Alexa" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1393730599p2/1894085.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/430772977?book_show_action=true">Oct 09, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Alexa" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Alexa" href="/user/show/1894085-alexa">Alexa</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781478172963" href="/book/show/15852521-the-vincent-brothers">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1894085-alexa?shelf=2012-reads">2012-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1894085-alexa?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1894085-alexa?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1894085-alexa?shelf=own">own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1894085-alexa?shelf=contemp-challenge">contemp-challenge</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer430772977" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10553357397858178795"><br/>My review can also be found on my blog <a href='http://collections-books.blogspot.com/2012/10/review-vincent-brothers-by-abbi-glines.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>Collections</a>.<br/><br/>I have to admit that The Vincent Boys novels weren't on my radar of books I desperately needed to read. But then I got my hands on copies of both and decided, <i>Why not?</i> They weren't long, and I was in the mood for something quick to read. It took me about 80 pages to finally get hooked into the first book The Vincent Boys. Once that happened I couldn't stop reading, and it ended up being a fun and enjoyable read for me. I was pleasantly surprised</span>
  <span id="freeText10553357397858178795" style="display:none"><br />My review can also be found on my blog <a href="http://collections-books.blogspot.com/2012/10/review-vincent-brothers-by-abbi-glines.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Collections</a>.<br /><br />I have to admit that The Vincent Boys novels weren't on my radar of books I desperately needed to read. But then I got my hands on copies of both and decided, <i>Why not?</i> They weren't long, and I was in the mood for something quick to read. It took me about 80 pages to finally get hooked into the first book The Vincent Boys. Once that happened I couldn't stop reading, and it ended up being a fun and enjoyable read for me. I was pleasantly surprised.<br /><br />Needless to say I was super pumped and VERY curious about the second book The Vincent Brothers. Actually even before finishing The Vincent Boys, I had this strange desire to read it and had a feeling that I would like it more than its predecessor. Characters like Lana, who was introduced in the first novel, are ones that I always find myself rooting for. She was the underdog. A sweet girl with a huge crush on a guy who never seemed to notice her and was in love with someone else. I wanted to know how she would win Sawyer's heart. With the way The Vincent Boys ended, it almost seemed like it would be a piece of cake! I seriously was not prepared for what happened in The Vincent Brothers.<br /><br />Sawyer left an impression in the previous novel but not a big one. He was the good, perfect boy. While I tend to like the nice guy, Sawyer seemed a bit too perfect. It was like he was hiding behind a facade. I felt that what happened between him and Ashton and Beau really gave him a chance to bring out his personality. He wasn't as clueless as he appeared to be, nor was he always a nice person. He could get angry and feel just as strongly as everyone else. I was still shocked when I began reading The Vincent Brothers though. After six months, I thought he would surely be over Ashton, but he was a lot more angrier and bitter. The way he acted towards Beau and Ashton's relationship and how he treated Lana (thankfully she knows how to stick up for herself!) in some instances made me wish someone would kick his ass. But I have to say that it made him a much more complex and interesting character, which is something I like to find in characters.<br /><br />Ashton and Beau have a hot relationship, but the romance between Lana and Sawyer... It was SIZZLING! It was definitely more amped up compared to the first book. And Sawyer may not be as experienced as Beau, but man, does he learn quickly! Lana and Sawyer's chemistry was off the charts, and even though Sawyer wasn't quite over Ashton, it was clear just how much he wanted Lana. I was seriously fanning myself at some parts and felt like passing out over how extremely hot it got. Their moments together were my favorite in the book. I couldn't get enough of them. I just loved it! And I would totally go on and on about them, but I don't want to spoil it all for those who haven't read it yet.<br /><br />The Vincent Brothers was a guilty pleasure read for me. It was completely addicting! I was hooked from the very beginning and stayed up long past my bedtime to finish it. I'm surprised by how much I adored this book and so very glad I gave it a chance. Lana and Sawyer were awesome characters, the story was fast-paced and intriguing, and the drama surprisingly gave it depth. It was enjoyable and fun, and honestly I wish it didn't have to end! If you love contemporaries with HOT romance and a lot of drama, I recommend you check out The Vincent Boys and The Vincent Brothers!</span>
  <a data-text-id="10553357397858178795" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('LXMt9BAEOfFozTzrz5G5ecvSsPUNgrKUSGrz6MEMewJQUdAfRf5/MTuLODf6A5cFXkx1PaVTRtK3q/c03oOWeQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('x69pwo6kjoWW3gXIXfxam4cD6Mu+BKSaHXLlxy2rv1C6jZQp217IRcWYARRobnTnEp0tAxbVUNzis+EbMiRSKw==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer17349349812292987863">Abbi Glines is a #1 New York Times, USA Today, and Wall Street Journal bestselling author of the Rosemary Beach, Sea Breeze, Vincent Boys, Field Party and Existence series. She never cooks unless baking during the Christmas holiday counts. She believes in ghosts and has a habit of asking people if their house is haunted before she goes in it. She drinks afternoon tea because she wants to be Britis</span>
  <span id="freeText17349349812292987863" style="display:none">Abbi Glines is a #1 New York Times, USA Today, and Wall Street Journal bestselling author of the Rosemary Beach, Sea Breeze, Vincent Boys, Field Party and Existence series. She never cooks unless baking during the Christmas holiday counts. She believes in ghosts and has a habit of asking people if their house is haunted before she goes in it. She drinks afternoon tea because she wants to be British but alas she was born in Alabama. When asked how many books she has written she has to stop and count on her fingers. When she’s not locked away writing, she is reading, shopping (major shoe and purse addiction), sneaking off to the movies alone, and listening to the drama in her teenagers lives while making mental notes on the good stuff to use later. Don’t judge.<br /><br />You can connect with Abbi online in several different ways. She uses social media to procrastinate.<br /></span>
